253b4(ka): yengs khyab byoed brel dad cen na'ang / gsung du ban gyi ds gno' bsdu bgrigs byed pa'o ga skabs kyi thad spug de tsam byung med pas/ 'di'i phyogs la nyams myeng dang lag len segs la lig zhes len gni dken pas / 
253b5(ka): gam cha gsad du yin pa dang / shes su de zhus bgrigs pa che yang mkhyen dpyed dab 'byams pa min chad/ 'doi' thad mthun rkyen zung la 'gal rkyen mang ba'i gseb ru dul brling 'grog pa dang la byung na/ phyegs gang sa'i / 
253b6(ka): thed yug dang gnas sangs tshad las brgal ba'i legs ma nig then thabs med pas/ de lugs kyis rjes su gzigs mthan rnal pas 'di la dog rkyen thad ye bsrang yong nges gnang de me zhing / 'di yi byas pa 'dis kyang sad /
